{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-05-19 22:56:04","updatedTime":"2021-05-19 22:56:04","title":"How to Capture Motion Blur in Photography (6 Tips)","link":"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-capture-motion-blur-in-photography/","description":"<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-capture-motion-blur-in-photography/\">How to Capture Motion Blur in Photography (6 Tips)</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. It was authored by <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/author/darren/\">Darren Rowse</a>.</p>\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209403\" style=\"width:1164px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1164px; padding-top:103.09%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1164\" height=\"1200\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/capture-motion-blur-photography-1005.jpg?resize=1164%2C1200&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"capture motion blur in photography\" class=\"wp-image-209403\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/capture-motion-blur-photography-1005.jpg?w=1164&#38;ssl=1 1164w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/capture-motion-blur-photography-1005.jpg?resize=291%2C300&#38;ssl=1 291w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/capture-motion-blur-photography-1005.jpg?resize=582%2C600&#38;ssl=1 582w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/capture-motion-blur-photography-1005.jpg?resize=768%2C792&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/capture-motion-blur-photography-1005.jpg?resize=717%2C739&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Are you looking to capture motion blur in your photography?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>While photographing motion blur might seem difficult, it&#8217;s actually pretty easy; with a bit of camera know-how, you&#8217;ll be taking stunning photos like a pro.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208301\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.93%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1004\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-1.jpg?resize=1500%2C1004&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"capture motion blur photography\" class=\"wp-image-208301\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-1.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-1.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-1.jpg?resize=600%2C402&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-1.jpg?resize=768%2C514&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-1.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-1.jpg?resize=436%2C293&#38;ssl=1 436w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-1.jpg?resize=717%2C480&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And that&#8217;s what this article is all about: giving you the tools and techniques you need to get beautiful results!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Note that motion blur can look great in any photography genre, so don&#8217;t try to limit yourself. Instead, embrace the power of the blur!</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"slow-down-your-shutter-speed\">1. Slow down your shutter speed</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Here&#8217;s the <em>fundamental </em>motion blur tip:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Use a <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/shutter-speed/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"slow shutter speed (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">slow shutter speed</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You see, the reason for motion blur is simply that your camera&#8217;s shutter remains open for a significant period of time. In other words: you get motion blur when your shutter speed is long, whereas you freeze the action when your shutter speed is short.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So the number one tip for capturing movement is to select a longer shutter speed.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208302\" style=\"width:998px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:998px; padding-top:150.3%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"998\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-4.jpg?resize=998%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"motion blur in front of buildings\" class=\"wp-image-208302\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-4.jpg?w=998&#38;ssl=1 998w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-4.jpg?resize=200%2C300&#38;ssl=1 200w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-4.jpg?resize=399%2C600&#38;ssl=1 399w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-4.jpg?resize=768%2C1154&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-4.jpg?resize=717%2C1078&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 998px) 100vw, 998px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>If your shutter speed is too fast (e.g., 1/4000s), you&#8217;re not going to capture much movement. But if you dial in a lengthy shutter speed (e.g., five seconds) you won&#8217;t need your subject to move much at all before you start to see blur.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>How long should your shutter speed be? Here, the speed of your <em>subject </em>comes into play. A moving snail and a moving racecar will give you very different results at the same shutter speed. The slower your subject, the slower the shutter speed needs to be to create blur.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The other factor that comes into play when determining shutter speed is how much light exists in the scene. A longer shutter speed lets more light into your camera and runs the risk of blowing out or overexposing your image. Below, we&#8217;ll cover some ways to let less light in (so you can use long shutter speeds <em>without </em>overexposure concerns).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Bottom line:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>There&#8217;s no <em>one-size-fits-all </em>shutter speed for motion blur. It&#8217;ll depend on the speed of your subject, the brightness of the scene, and how much motion blur you want to capture. The key is to experiment!</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"stabilize-your-camera\">2. Stabilize your camera</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>There are two ways to get a feeling of motion in your images:</p>\n\n\n\n<ol><li>Have your subject move.</li><li>Have your camera move.</li></ol>\n\n\n\n<p>But for the type of photo we&#8217;re after today, it&#8217;ll be the <em>subject </em>that&#8217;s moving. In such cases, you need to do everything you can to keep your camera perfectly still. Otherwise, you&#8217;ll capture a blurry subject &#8211; but you&#8217;ll also end up with a blurry background.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>How do you stabilize your camera?</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208311\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:58.13%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"872\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-8-1.jpg?resize=1500%2C872&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"boats in the water\" class=\"wp-image-208311\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-8-1.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-8-1.jpg?resize=300%2C174&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-8-1.jpg?resize=600%2C349&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-8-1.jpg?resize=768%2C446&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-8-1.jpg?resize=717%2C417&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>A tripod is ideal, but you can also place your camera on some other steady object (e.g., a table or a bench). I&#8217;d recommend using a <a aria-label=\"remote shutter release or a self-timer mechanism (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/remote-shutter-vs-delayed-shutter/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">remote shutter release or a self-timer mechanism</a>; that way, you can trigger the shutter <em>without </em>touching your camera (because the more you touch your camera, the more likely it is that you&#8217;ll introduce blur).</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"try-shutter-priority-mode\">3. Try Shutter Priority mode</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>As you know, the shutter speed is crucial to achieving a beautiful blurred look. Even small changes will have a big impact upon your shot &#8211; so you should use a camera mode that gives you full control over your camera&#8217;s shutter.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You have two options. First, you can switch your camera to full <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/shoot-manual-mode-cheat-sheet-beginners/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"Manual mode (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Manual mode</a>. It&#8217;ll work well, and it&#8217;s a good idea for more experienced photographers &#8211; but in Manual mode, you&#8217;ll also need to select your <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/aperture/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"aperture (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">aperture</a> and <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/iso-settings/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"ISO (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">ISO</a> (and you&#8217;ll need to make sure that the shutter speed, aperture, and ISO interact to create a perfect exposure). So if you don&#8217;t yet feel confident working in Manual mode, you have another option:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/aperture-and-shutter-priority-modes/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"Shutter Priority mode (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Shutter Priority mode</a>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>With Shutter Priority, <em>you </em>set the shutter speed (and the ISO, if you so choose), but your camera will set the aperture to ensure the shot is well exposed. It&#8217;s a very handy mode for motion blur photography because it ensures you get the movement effect you&#8217;re after while <em>also </em>capturing generally well-exposed images.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208308\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-7.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"motorcyclist motion blur photography\" class=\"wp-image-208308\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-7.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-7.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-7.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-7.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-7.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-7.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"how-to-compensate-for-long-shutter-speeds-when-there-is-too-much-light\">How to compensate for long shutter speeds when there is too much light</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Remember what I said about a long shutter speed?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The longer the speed, the more light that will get into your camera, and the brighter your photos will be. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So unless you compensate for this, whenever you try to capture motion blur, you&#8217;ll end up with overexposed shots.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Below, I&#8217;ll suggest three easy methods for preventing this overexposure. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>(Note: A fourth method is to simply wait for the light to change &#8211; i.e., for it to get darker. Many shots that incorporate blur are taken at night or at dawn/dusk for this reason.)</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"use-a-small-aperture\">1. Use a small aperture</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Here&#8217;s the first, and simplest, method of preventing overexposure:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Narrow the aperture. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Because the narrower the aperture, the less light that will hit the camera sensor. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you&#8217;re shooting in Shutter Priority, your camera will actually narrow the aperture for you. As soon as it detects a slow shutter speed, it&#8217;ll close down the aperture and deliver a well-exposed shot.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But if you&#8217;re shooting in Manual mode or Aperture Priority, the aperture can generally be changed via a dial on your camera.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>One thing to bear in mind:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Adjusting the aperture won&#8217;t <em>just </em>affect your photo&#8217;s exposure. Aperture also affects the <em><a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/understanding-depth-field-beginners/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">depth of field</a></em>, which refers to the amount of the scene that&#8217;s sharp. A wide aperture creates a limited depth of field, like this:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208303\" style=\"width:1200px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1200px; padding-top:125%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-6-1.jpg?resize=1200%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"watch with spinning hands capture motion blur photography\" class=\"wp-image-208303\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-6-1.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-6-1.jpg?resize=240%2C300&#38;ssl=1 240w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-6-1.jpg?resize=480%2C600&#38;ssl=1 480w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-6-1.jpg?resize=768%2C960&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-6-1.jpg?resize=717%2C896&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Whereas a narrow aperture ensures the entire scene is sharp throughout:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208304\" style=\"width:1001px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1001px; padding-top:149.85%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1001\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-3-1.jpg?resize=1001%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"capture motion blur photography car driving\" class=\"wp-image-208304\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-3-1.jpg?w=1001&#38;ssl=1 1001w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-3-1.jpg?resize=200%2C300&#38;ssl=1 200w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-3-1.jpg?resize=400%2C600&#38;ssl=1 400w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-3-1.jpg?resize=768%2C1151&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-3-1.jpg?resize=717%2C1074&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>So while it&#8217;s easy to combine a deep depth of field with a well-exposed motion blur image, working with a shallow depth of field while <em>also </em>ensuring well-exposed motion blur can be tough. If you&#8217;re after a shallow depth of field effect, you&#8217;ll need to counteract overexposure another way, as I explain in the next section:</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"decrease-your-iso\">2. Decrease your ISO</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>If you&#8217;ve tried narrowing your aperture and still aren&#8217;t getting you the results you need, or if you&#8217;re after a shallow depth of field, here&#8217;s an alternative method for preventing overexposure:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Drop your ISO.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>ISO impacts the sensitivity of your digital camera&#8217;s sensor to light, where a higher number will induce <em>greater </em>sensitivity (and therefore a brighter exposure) and a lower number will induce <em>less </em>sensitivity (and therefore a darker exposure). </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208307\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:74.87%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1123\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-10.jpg?resize=1500%2C1123&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"train moving fast with platform\" class=\"wp-image-208307\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-10.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-10.jpg?resize=300%2C225&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-10.jpg?resize=600%2C449&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-10.jpg?resize=768%2C575&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-10.jpg?resize=717%2C537&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>You can adjust your ISO in Manual mode or Shutter Priority mode, so simply dial in a low ISO (such as 100) and watch as your exposure decreases. Of course, there&#8217;s a limit to how low you can drop your ISO; once you get to ISO 100 or ISO 50, your camera won&#8217;t allow you to go any further. But it&#8217;s always worth checking whether a lower ISO is an option because it&#8217;s a simple way to prevent overexposure.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"try-a-neutral-density-filter\">3. Try a neutral density filter</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Say you&#8217;re after a motion blur photo, but you just can&#8217;t get the exposure dark enough. You&#8217;ve narrowed the aperture, you&#8217;ve dropped the ISO, but your shots keep coming out overexposed. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>You still have another, more dedicated option:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>A <a aria-label=\"neutral density filter (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/neutral-density-filters-landscape-photos/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">neutral density filter</a>. It&#8217;s a piece of glass that blocks light from passing through your lens &#8211; sort of like sunglasses &#8211; and lets you use a <em>long </em>shutter speed while preventing overexposure. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>For example, if you&#8217;re shooting a seascape in bright sunlight and you want to blur the water, you&#8217;ll end up with a blown-out, overexposed scene &#8211; even with a narrow aperture and low ISO. But pop a neutral density filter over your lens, and you can slow the shutter speed right down while keeping a perfect exposure.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208305\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-5-1.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"long exposure seascape blur\" class=\"wp-image-208305\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-5-1.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-5-1.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-5-1.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-5-1.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-5-1.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-5-1.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>(By the way, a <em><a aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-use-and-buy-polarizing-filters/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">polarizing filter</a> </em>can have a similar effect, though it&#8217;ll also impact the look of your images by cutting out reflections.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Note that neutral density filters come in many strengths. You can get a basic, subtle ND filter, one that&#8217;ll slightly darken the scene. Or you can buy an ultra-powerful, 10-stop ND filter, which will allow you to dramatically lengthen your shutter speed in bright sunlight.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"a-quick-note-two-more-creative-techniques-to-try\">A quick note: two more creative techniques to try</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>If you want to capture images with motion blur but you&#8217;re looking to come away with uniquely artistic results, here are two other techniques to consider:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a aria-label=\"Slow sync flash (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/slow-sync-flash/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Slow sync flash</a>. This lets you capture a relatively sharp subject while creating a moving, blurry background, and it&#8217;s a great way to create in-your-face shots.</li><li><a aria-label=\"Panning (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/mastering-panning-to-photograph-moving-subjects/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Panning</a>. Here, you simply follow a moving subject with your camera; the subject will generally come out nice and sharp, while the background stretches and blurs.</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208306\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.73%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1001\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-9.jpg?resize=1500%2C1001&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"panning with motorcycle\" class=\"wp-image-208306\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-9.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-9.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-9.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-9.jpg?resize=768%2C513&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-9.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-9.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"motion-blur-in-photography-conclusion\">Motion blur in photography: conclusion</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Well, there you have it! Six easy tips to capture motion blur in photography.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So remember these tips. And the next time you&#8217;re after some creative motion blur photos, you&#8217;ll get stunning results!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now over to you:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>Have you tried taking motion blur photos? Did it go well? Do you have any tricks or tips? Share your thoughts (and images!) in the comments below!</em></p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208310\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-2.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"capture motion blur photography racecar\" class=\"wp-image-208310\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-2.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-2.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-2.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-2.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-2.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/motion-blur-photography-2.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-capture-motion-blur-in-photography/\">How to Capture Motion Blur in Photography (6 Tips)</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\" class=\"ek-link\">SonyAlphaRumors</a> has been dropping information regarding the so-called Sony a6900, which will debut in “late May” as an <a href=\"https://geni.us/SonyA6600camera\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"a6600 (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">a6600</a> successor.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>While the “a6900” moniker is not yet confirmed, a “trusted” SonyAlphaRumors source has said that the new camera “will not be named ‘a6700,’” with another SAR source offering the a6900 label.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So what do we know about this new a6900?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>SonyAlphaRumors confidently states that the a6900 will replace the a6600, but will feature an <a aria-label=\"APS-C sensor (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/camera-sensors-explained/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">APS-C sensor</a> and a body similar to the full-frame <a aria-label=\"a7C (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://geni.us/Sonya7CDPS\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">a7C</a>. It will “be branded as [a] ‘vlogger’ camera,” which suggests several blogging-friendly specs: a fully articulating screen, for one, but also impressive video capabilities (at <em>least </em>4K/30p plus mic/headphone jacks) and a compact design.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image is-style-with-caption\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209209\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:75%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1125\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/Sony-a6900-release-2.jpg?resize=1500%2C1125&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Sony a6900 release\" class=\"wp-image-209209\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/Sony-a6900-release-2.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/Sony-a6900-release-2.jpg?resize=300%2C225&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/Sony-a6900-release-2.jpg?resize=600%2C450&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/Sony-a6900-release-2.jpg?resize=768%2C576&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/Sony-a6900-release-2.jpg?resize=717%2C538&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span><figcaption>The Sony a6900 will look much like the compact a7C.</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Indeed, <a aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.sonyalpharumors.com/rumor-first-possible-sony-a6700-specs-new-32mp-sensor-4k60p-v-log-focused-camera-like-the-zv-1/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\" class=\"ek-link\">various rumors</a> suggest that the a6900 will feature 4K/60p video, a notable upgrade over the 4K/30p offered by the a6600. Interestingly, rumors also point to a new high-resolution sensor &#8211; several SonyAlphaRumors sources have suggested 32 MP &#8211; in a surprising break from Sony’s string of <a aria-label=\"24 MP APS-C models (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/which-sony-a6000-series-camera-should-you-buy/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">24 MP APS-C models</a>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Here are additional specs suggested by (unconfirmed) SAR sources:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Improved rolling shutter performance</li><li>20 frames-per-second continuous shooting</li><li>2.36M-dot EVF</li><li>The “same tilt screen” as the a7C</li><li>Upgraded in-body image stabilization (compared to the a7C)</li><li>A7C-like price ($1798 USD)</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>Most of these items seem pretty standard and don’t offer any major improvements over the a6600. The exception is the 20 fps continuous shooting rate, and I’ll admit that I’m skeptical; after all, it’s a feature matched only by Sony’s highest-level full-frame models and is wholly unnecessary for vloggers.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Of course, you can also expect Sony’s standard <a aria-label=\"autofocusing (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/focus-on-autofocus/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">autofocusing</a> capabilities, including its vaunted Real-time Eye AF, plus outstanding subject tracking and generally speedy focusing, all of which will appeal to vloggers and still shooters alike.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So be sure to keep an eye out for further Sony a6900 news, especially if you’re interested in a compact, vlogging-focused camera; we should get an official release before the month is out.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now over to you:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>What do you think of the Sony a6900? If the rumored specifications are right, would you be interested? Are there any key features that the camera is missing? <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-batch-resize-in-photoshop/\">How to Batch Resize in Photoshop: A Step-by-Step Guide (2021)</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. It was authored by <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/author/hbradley/\">Helen Bradley</a>.</p>\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208983\" style=\"width:1200px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1200px; padding-top:100%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1200\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1001.jpg?resize=1200%2C1200&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to batch resize in Photoshop: a guide\" class=\"wp-image-208983\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1001.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1001.jpg?resize=300%2C300&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1001.jpg?resize=600%2C600&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1001.jpg?resize=150%2C150&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1001.jpg?resize=768%2C768&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1001.jpg?resize=717%2C717&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1001.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>What&#8217;s the easiest way to batch resize in Photoshop? </p>\n\n\n\n<p>In this article, I&#8217;m going to take you through a simple, step-by-step process for resizing your images. It&#8217;ll take <em>seconds </em>&#8211; and when you&#8217;re done, you&#8217;ll be able to resize dozens (or hundreds!) of photos at once.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Let&#8217;s get started.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"batch-resizing-in-photoshop-step-by-step\">Batch resizing in Photoshop: step by step</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Batch resizing isn&#8217;t hard, and it takes very little knowledge. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>To start, make sure you open <em>some</em> files in Photoshop (though note that you don&#8217;t need to open all the files you&#8217;re aiming to resize; a random file or an empty canvas will do just fine). As you can see below, I&#8217;ve opened a blank document:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208966\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:64.13%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"962\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-14.jpg?resize=1500%2C962&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"a blank canvas in Photoshop\" class=\"wp-image-208966\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-14.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-14.jpg?resize=300%2C192&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-14.jpg?resize=600%2C385&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-14.jpg?resize=768%2C493&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-14.jpg?resize=115%2C75&#38;ssl=1 115w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-14.jpg?resize=717%2C460&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>I&#8217;m going to cover the <em>Image Processor </em>method of batch resizing. Pretty much anyone can do it, and it generally works well. However, if you have more complex batch resizing requirements, consider <a aria-label=\"writing an action (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-create-and-use-photoshop-actions-to-speed-up-your-workflow/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">writing an action</a>; that way, you can tailor the resizing to your particular needs. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now let&#8217;s take a closer look at the batch resizing process, starting with:</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-open-the-image-processor\">Step 1: Open the Image Processor</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Choose <strong>File&#62;Scripts&#62;Image Processor</strong>. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208967\" style=\"width:1108px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1108px; padding-top:108.94%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1108\" height=\"1207\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-15.jpg?resize=1108%2C1207&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting the Image Processor option\" class=\"wp-image-208967\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-15.jpg?w=1108&#38;ssl=1 1108w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-15.jpg?resize=275%2C300&#38;ssl=1 275w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-15.jpg?resize=551%2C600&#38;ssl=1 551w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-15.jpg?resize=768%2C837&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-15.jpg?resize=717%2C781&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>The Image Processor dialog box will open, where you&#8217;ll see a simple, four-step process for resizing your images:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208968\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-16.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"the Image Processor dialog box\" class=\"wp-image-208968\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-16.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-16.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-16.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-16.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-16.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-16.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-select-your-images-for-batch-resizing\">Step 2: Select your images for batch resizing</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>In the first section of the Image Processor dialog box, you&#8217;ll need to identify the images you want to batch resize. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>You can choose to resize all open images by selecting <strong>Use Open Images</strong>:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208969\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to batch resize in Photoshop choosing the images\" class=\"wp-image-208969\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-1.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Or you can pick a folder from your hard drive via the <strong>Select Folder </strong>button:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208970\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-2.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"choosing the images to batch resize\" class=\"wp-image-208970\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-2.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-2.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-2.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-2.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-2.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-2.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>If you do select a folder, you can tell Photoshop to resize images in all subfolders as well; just hit the <strong>Include All sub-folders </strong>checkbox:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208971\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-3.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting the Include All sub-folders option\" class=\"wp-image-208971\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-3.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-3.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-3.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-3.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-3.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-3.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-determine-your-export-location\">Step 3: Determine your export location</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Now it&#8217;s time to determine where you want your resized images to go. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>To save the resized versions alongside the originals, simply select <strong>Save in Same Location</strong>:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208972\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-4.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting the location for the resized images\" class=\"wp-image-208972\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-4.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-4.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-4.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-4.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-4.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-4.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then, when the resizing begins, Photoshop will create a subfolder next to the original files. (Because your resized versions will retain the names of the original files, creating a subfolder &#8211; rather than simply saving the images in the original folder &#8211; prevents any overwriting.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Alternatively, you can select a different folder for the resized files:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208973\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-6.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"choosing an export location\" class=\"wp-image-208973\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-6.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-6.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-6.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-6.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-6.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-6.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-input-your-preferred-image-sizes\">Step 4: Input your preferred image sizes</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>This is the most important step of the entire process:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The moment where you dial in resize settings for your files. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>First, determine your output file type. You can choose from <a aria-label=\"JPEG, PSD, and TIFF (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/what-is-the-best-file-format-to-save-your-photos-in-psd-tiff-jpeg-gif%C2%A0-png/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">JPEG, PSD, and TIFF</a> (JPEG is the default and generally works well, but if you&#8217;re working with layered files, then PSD is a good choice).</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208974\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-7.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting Save as JPEG\" class=\"wp-image-208974\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-7.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-7.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-7.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-7.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-7.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-7.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>If you do decide to save JPEGs, you can adjust the output quality; 12 will give you large, great-looking photos, whereas 1 will give you tiny, low-quality results. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>For better color when displaying your photos on the web, select <strong>Convert Profile to sRGB</strong>:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208975\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-8.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting Convert Profile to sRGB\" class=\"wp-image-208975\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-8.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-8.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-8.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-8.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-8.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-8.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>I also recommend checking the <strong>Include ICC Profile </strong>box at the bottom:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208976\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-9.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting Include ICC Profile\" class=\"wp-image-208976\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-9.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-9.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-9.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-9.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-9.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-9.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Finally, select <strong>Resize to Fit</strong>, and type in your preferred file size!</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208986\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-10.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting Resize to Fit \" class=\"wp-image-208986\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-10.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-10.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-10.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-10.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-10.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-10.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Note that the dimensions you dial in are <em>maximums</em>. So if you type in 300 for the width and 300 for the height, the files will be resized so that the longest side of every image is 300 pixels. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>(In other words, the images won&#8217;t be <em>cropped </em>or <em>skewed </em>to fit your preferred dimensions; they&#8217;ll be scaled up or down for the most natural-looking results.)</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208978\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-11.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to batch resize in Photoshop typing in a width and height\" class=\"wp-image-208978\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-11.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-11.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-11.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-11.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-11.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-11.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Also note that the width and height measurements don&#8217;t have to be the same. You could specify a width of 400 and a height of 300 &#8211; then all images would be constrained to a width of 400 or a height of 300, whichever comes first. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>By the way, you do have the option to save your images in a second (or third) format, as well. Just select the <strong>Save as PSD </strong>or <strong>Save as TIFF </strong>checkboxes, and PSD and/or TIFF folders will be created alongside your JPEG folder! </p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-run-the-script\">Step 5: Run the script</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>When you’re ready, click <strong>Run</strong>. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208979\" style=\"width:925px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:925px; padding-top:97.95%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"925\" height=\"906\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-12.jpg?resize=925%2C906&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"hit the Run button\" class=\"wp-image-208979\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-12.jpg?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-12.jpg?resize=300%2C294&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-12.jpg?resize=600%2C588&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-12.jpg?resize=768%2C752&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-12.jpg?resize=717%2C702&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-12.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 925px) 100vw, 925px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>The images will be automatically opened (if they&#8217;re not open already), resized, saved, and closed again.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>To find your resized images, simply head to the folder you specified in <strong>Step 3 </strong>(above). If you chose to save JPEGs, the images will be in a subfolder called <strong>JPEG</strong>; if you chose to save TIFFs, the images will be in a subfolder called <strong>TIFF</strong>, etc.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Like this:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208980\" style=\"width:1466px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1466px; padding-top:47.2%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1466\" height=\"692\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-19.jpg?resize=1466%2C692&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"finding the resized photos\" class=\"wp-image-208980\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-19.jpg?w=1466&#38;ssl=1 1466w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-19.jpg?resize=300%2C142&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-19.jpg?resize=600%2C283&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-19.jpg?resize=768%2C363&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-19.jpg?resize=717%2C338&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"how-to-batch-resize-in-photoshop-final-words\">How to batch resize in Photoshop: final words</h2>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-208965\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:65.47%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"982\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-13-1.jpg?resize=1500%2C982&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to batch resize in Photoshop\" class=\"wp-image-208965\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-13-1.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-13-1.jpg?resize=300%2C196&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-13-1.jpg?resize=600%2C393&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-13-1.jpg?resize=768%2C503&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-13-1.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-13-1.jpg?resize=115%2C75&#38;ssl=1 115w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-batch-resize-in-Photoshop-13-1.jpg?resize=717%2C469&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Well, there you have it:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The easiest way to batch resize your images in Photoshop. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So whenever you need to resize a lot of images for uploading on the web, use the Photoshop Image Processor. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>It makes the job quick and painless!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now over to you:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>Do you have a favorite method of batch resizing images in Photoshop? If so, share it in the comments below!</em></p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-batch-resize-in-photoshop/\">How to Batch Resize in Photoshop: A Step-by-Step Guide (2021)</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>.
