97cf891ab06100.webp","https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/04/OziRig_Rhino_CA_Recrop.jpg?ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn87@2020_5/2021/05/19/14-56-36-502_94175e4220a4a4ed.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/DigitalPhotographySchool?i=rEPnCv_y1GI:FmZBJpPsSfk:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn29@2020_3/2021/05/19/14-56-35-320_d0ce2083e88c9466.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/DigitalPhotographySchool?d=7Q72WNTAKBA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn38@2020_6/2021/05/19/14-56-36-551_849a6e90690e7208.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/DigitalPhotographySchool?d=ByNYXvuKCJE":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn68@2020_1/2021/05/19/14-56-35-216_7752f86734b1d8c8.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/DigitalPhotographySchool?i=rEPnCv_y1GI:FmZBJpPsSfk:guobEISWfyQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn39@2020_2/2021/05/19/14-56-35-210_7f1bf74579426ea6.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/DigitalPhotographySchool/~4/rEPnCv_y1GI":null},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1621436164667},{"createdTime":"2021-05-19 22:56:04","updatedTime":"2021-05-19 22:56:04","title":"How to Take Great Group Photos: 12 Easy Tips","link":"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-take-great-group-photos/","description":"<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-take-great-group-photos/\">How to Take Great Group Photos: 12 Easy Tips</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. It was authored by <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/author/darren/\">Darren Rowse</a>.</p>\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209264\" style=\"width:1200px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1200px; padding-top:100%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1200\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/group-photography-tips-1005-1.jpg?resize=1200%2C1200&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to take group photos\" class=\"wp-image-209264\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/group-photography-tips-1005-1.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/group-photography-tips-1005-1.jpg?resize=300%2C300&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/group-photography-tips-1005-1.jpg?resize=600%2C600&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/group-photography-tips-1005-1.jpg?resize=150%2C150&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/group-photography-tips-1005-1.jpg?resize=768%2C768&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/group-photography-tips-1005-1.jpg?resize=717%2C717&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/group-photography-tips-1005-1.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>If you&#8217;re looking to take beautiful group photos, you&#8217;ve come to the right place. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>In this article, I&#8217;m going to share 12 simple tips for capturing stunning photos of groups. Specifically, I&#8217;ll discuss:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>How to pose a group like a pro</li><li>A simple trick to capture <em>everyone </em>in the group looking their best</li><li>How to pick the perfect group photo location</li><li>Much, much more!</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>So if you&#8217;re ready to become a group photography expert, then let&#8217;s get started!</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"prepare-ahead-of-time\">1. Prepare ahead of time</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>There is <em>nothing </em>that will make group photo subjects turn on you faster than you not being prepared. People don&#8217;t like to be kept waiting, so plan ahead.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Here&#8217;s what I recommend you do several hours (or days) before the photo:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Scope out the location of your shot beforehand</li><li>Think about how you will <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/posing-guide-21-sample-poses-to-get-you-started-with-photographing-groups-of-people/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">pose people</a> and frame your shot</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>Then, a few minutes before the photo:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Make sure everyone you want in the shot <em>knows </em>that you want them in the shot</li><li>Make sure your camera is on and has charged batteries</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205429\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-4-1.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to take group photos three women\" class=\"wp-image-205429\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-4-1.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-4-1.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-4-1.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-4-1.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-4-1.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-4-1.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"carefully-choose-the-location\">2. Carefully choose the location</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>The group photo <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-choose-a-great-portrait-photography-location/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"location (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">location</a> is important for a number of reasons. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>First, it can give the photo context. For example, a shot of a sports team on their playing field says more than a shot of the team in front of a brick wall. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Second, the location can help emphasize your group &#8211; or it can draw the eye. To make the group stand out, you&#8217;ll need a location with no distractions.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So choose a place where your group will fit, where there is enough light for the shot, and where there are no distracting surroundings. Also, avoid setting up a group shot directly in front of a window where the light from your flash might reflect back in an unpleasant way. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205426\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-1.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"group posing on a mountain\" class=\"wp-image-205426\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-1.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-1.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-1.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-1.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-1.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-1.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"take-multiple-shots\">3. Take multiple shots</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Sometimes, it&#8217;s tough to get <em>everyone</em> looking just right at the exact same time. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>That&#8217;s why I highly recommend you take multiple photos quickly; I often switch my camera to <a aria-label=\"continuous shooting mode (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/burst-mode/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">continuous shooting mode</a> and photograph in short bursts. The first shot is often no good &#8211; but the shot or two directly after gives a group that looks less posed and more relaxed.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>On a related note, shoot some frames before everyone is ready. Sometimes, the organization of a group shot can be quite comical and image-worthy (as people tell each other where to go and jostle for position).</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205428\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-7.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"kids in a group waving\" class=\"wp-image-205428\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-7.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-7.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-7.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-7.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-7.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-7.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Also, mix up the framing of your shots a little. If you have a zoom lens, try capturing some shots at a wide focal length and some shots that are more tightly framed.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"get-in-close\">4. Get in close</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Try to get as close as you can to the group you&#8217;re photographing (without cutting out group members, of course!). The closer you can get, the more detail you&#8217;ll capture in their faces &#8211; something that can really elevate a shot.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If your group is small, step in and take some <a aria-label=\"head and shoulder shots (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/10-tips-for-photographing-great-headshots/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">head and shoulder shots</a>. Another effective technique is to get everyone to lean in; that way, you can move even closer without cutting out subjects. You might also try moving everyone out of a one-line formation and placing some people in front and behind.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"pose-the-group\">5. Pose the group</h2>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-91223\" style=\"width:1280px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1280px; padding-top:75%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1280\" height=\"960\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/133823195_13dd92f2d6_o.jpg?resize=1280%2C960&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to take group photos people in uniforms looking up\" class=\"wp-image-91223\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/133823195_13dd92f2d6_o.jpg?w=1280&#38;ssl=1 1280w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/133823195_13dd92f2d6_o.jpg?resize=300%2C225&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/133823195_13dd92f2d6_o.jpg?resize=600%2C450&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/133823195_13dd92f2d6_o.jpg?resize=717%2C538&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>In most cases, your group will pose itself pretty naturally (after all, we&#8217;ve all been in a group shot at some point). Tall people will go to the back, short people to the front. But there are other things you can do to improve the photo&#8217;s composition: </p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>If the event is centered around one or two people (like a wedding or a birthday), make the hosts the focal point by putting them right in the middle of the group (you can add variation by taking some shots of everyone looking at the camera and other shots of everyone looking at the person/couple).</li><li>For formal group photos, put taller members toward the back <em>center </em>of the shot, with shorter people along the edges.</li><li>Try not to make the group too deep (i.e., keep the distance between the front line of people and the back line of people as small as you can). This will help keep everyone in focus. If the composition does end up being deep, use a narrow aperture.</li><li>Tell everyone to raise their chins a little; they&#8217;ll thank you later when they see the shot without any double chins!</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"time-your-group-shot-well\">6. Time your group shot well</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Carefully pick the moment for your photo. Try to choose a time that works with what is happening at the gathering. I find it best to do a group shot when people are already close together and when there is a lull in the proceedings. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>The start of an event can be a good time to shoot; everyone is together, they all look their best, and if there is alcohol involved, it hasn&#8217;t significantly affected the group yet. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205432\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:72.2%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1083\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-2-1.jpg?resize=1500%2C1083&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"girls on a hill\" class=\"wp-image-205432\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-2-1.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-2-1.jpg?resize=300%2C217&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-2-1.jpg?resize=600%2C433&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-2-1.jpg?resize=768%2C554&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-2-1.jpg?resize=717%2C518&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"think-about-the-light\">7. Think about the light </h2>\n\n\n\n<p>In order to get enough detail in the final shot, you need to have sufficient light. The way you should do this varies from situation to situation &#8211; but consider using a <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/starting-with-off-camera-flash-techniques/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"flash (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">flash</a> if the group is small enough and you are close enough for it to take effect, especially if the main source of light is coming from behind the group. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>If it&#8217;s a bright, sunny day and the sun is low in the sky, try not to face your subjects toward the light &#8211; otherwise, you&#8217;ll end up with a collection of squinting faces.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205433\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:56.27%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"844\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-6.jpg?resize=1500%2C844&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"group in the ocean\" class=\"wp-image-205433\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-6.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-6.jpg?resize=300%2C169&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-6.jpg?resize=600%2C338&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-6.jpg?resize=768%2C432&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-6.jpg?resize=717%2C403&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"take-control\">8. Take control</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>I&#8217;ve been in a number of group photos where the photographer almost lost control of their subjects. It happened for two reasons:</p>\n\n\n\n<ol><li>They weren&#8217;t quick enough.</li><li>They didn&#8217;t communicate well with the group.</li></ol>\n\n\n\n<p>When shooting a group photo, it&#8217;s important to keep talking, let the group know what you want them to do, motivate them to smile, tell them that they look great, and make clear how long you&#8217;ll need them for.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>It&#8217;s also important to give your subjects a reason to pose for the photograph (and to listen to you). At a wedding, you might motivate people by saying &#8220;The happy couple has asked me to get some group shots.&#8221; At a sporting event, you could say, &#8220;Let&#8217;s take a group photo to celebrate our win.&#8221; When you give people a reason to pose, you&#8217;ll find they are much more willing to stand for a few minutes while you snap photos.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Here&#8217;s another very useful line to use with a group: &#8220;If you can see the camera, then it can see you.&#8221; This one is key if you want to be able to see each person&#8217;s face in the final image. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>If there are other photographers, just wait until they&#8217;ve all finished their shots, then get the attention of the full group. Otherwise, you&#8217;ll get everyone looking in different directions.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Of course, you don&#8217;t want to be a dictator when posing your group &#8211; otherwise, your group shots will include some very angry expressions. The best photographers know how to get people&#8217;s attention and communicate what they want, while also keeping people relaxed and having fun.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205431\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-8.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to take group photos girls in a line\" class=\"wp-image-205431\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-8.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-8.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-8.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-8.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-8.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-8.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"get-up-high-when-photographing-large-groups\">9. Get up high when photographing large groups</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Large groups of people can be very difficult to photograph. Even with careful staggering and tiering, you&#8217;ll struggle to fit everyone into the shot.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>One solution is to <em>elevate </em>yourself. If I&#8217;m photographing a wedding and the couple wants one big group shot, I&#8217;ll arrange for a ladder to be present, or I&#8217;ll find some other way to get up high (I&#8217;ve even climbed up onto church roofs!). A high vantage point lets you fit a lot of people into the frame while still remaining quite close to the group. It also gives an interesting perspective, especially if you&#8217;re using a nice, wide focal length. </p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"use-a-tripod\">10. Use a tripod </h2>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205435\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.93%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1004\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-5.jpg?resize=1500%2C1004&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"kids posing for a group photo\" class=\"wp-image-205435\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-5.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-5.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-5.jpg?resize=600%2C402&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-5.jpg?resize=768%2C514&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-5.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-5.jpg?resize=436%2C293&#38;ssl=1 436w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-5.jpg?resize=717%2C480&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>There are a number of reasons why tripods are great for group photography. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>First, a tripod communicates your seriousness and can help get the group&#8217;s attention (it&#8217;s amazing what a professional-looking setup can do!).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Second, a tripod gives you more freedom to pose your subjects. Simply set your camera on a tripod, set the exposure, and set the focus. Then guide your subjects through different poses &#8211; and when everything looks just right, you can quickly press the shutter button!</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"use-an-assistant\">11. Use an assistant</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>If you have a very large group, an assistant can be super helpful. For one, they can get the group organized &#8211; tell people when to come, where to stand, etc.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>An assistant is also incredibly handy if you are taking multiple group shots (like at a wedding when you&#8217;re photographing different configurations of a family). In such a case, I often ask the couple to provide me with a family member or a friend who can ensure we have everyone we need in each shot.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Having a family member act as your assistant ensures you don&#8217;t miss anyone (assuming they&#8217;re related to members of the group). Plus, the group will be familiar with them and will therefore respond well when the &#8220;assistant&#8221; orders them around.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"smile\">12. Smile</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Yes, <em>you </em>should smile! During a group session, there&#8217;s nothing worse than a grumpy, stressed-out photographer. Have fun and enjoy the process of getting your shots, and you&#8217;ll find the group will, too. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>In fact, after photographing a wedding, I usually come home with an incredibly sore face from all the smiling I&#8217;ve done! I find the best way to get the couple and their family to relax and smile is to smile at them. It really does work. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205434\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-3.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"business group photo\" class=\"wp-image-205434\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-3.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-3.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-3.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-3.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-3.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-group-photos-3.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"bonus-tip-let-your-imagination-run-wild\">Bonus tip: Let your imagination run wild!</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>One more quick tip. Get a little creative! You don&#8217;t always have to use standard compositions; instead, you can capture more imaginative, <em>unusual </em>photos.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-205436\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-great-group-photos-9.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"women posing in a bathtub\" class=\"wp-image-205436\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-great-group-photos-9.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-great-group-photos-9.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-great-group-photos-9.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-great-group-photos-9.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-great-group-photos-9.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/how-to-take-great-group-photos-9.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"how-to-take-great-group-photos-conclusion\">How to take great group photos: conclusion</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Group photos might seem difficult, but they&#8217;re really not!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Just follow the tips I&#8217;ve given you, and your group photos will turn out <em>stunning</em>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now over to you:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>Have you had success taking group photos? Share your shots in the comments below!</em> <em>Also, if you enjoyed this article, <a aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/subscribe/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">subscribe to the dPS newsletter</a>!</em></p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-take-great-group-photos/\">How to Take Great Group Photos: 12 Easy Tips</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. 22:56:04","updatedTime":"2021-05-19 22:56:04","title":"How to Make a Photoshop Collage (in 9 Simple Steps)","link":"https://digital-photography-school.com/?p=81101","description":"<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/make-photoshop-collage-9-steps/\">How to Make a Photoshop Collage (in 9 Simple Steps)</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. It was authored by <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/author/nataliarobert/\">Natalia Robert</a>.</p>\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209058\" style=\"width:1200px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1200px; padding-top:100%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1200\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1003.jpg?resize=1200%2C1200&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how to make a Photoshop collage\" class=\"wp-image-209058\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1003.jpg?w=1200&#38;ssl=1 1200w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1003.jpg?resize=300%2C300&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1003.jpg?resize=600%2C600&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1003.jpg?resize=150%2C150&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1003.jpg?resize=768%2C768&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1003.jpg?resize=717%2C717&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1003.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Looking to make a collage in <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/5-easy-photoshop-tips-beginners/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Photoshop</a>? You&#8217;ve come to the right place. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>In this article, I&#8217;m going to give you an easy, step-by-step process for creating a stunning collage &#8211; one that looks like this:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209028\" style=\"width:994px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:994px; padding-top:137.02%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"994\" height=\"1362\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1001-1.jpg?resize=994%2C1362&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"final collage\" class=\"wp-image-209028\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1001-1.jpg?w=994&#38;ssl=1 994w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1001-1.jpg?resize=219%2C300&#38;ssl=1 219w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1001-1.jpg?resize=438%2C600&#38;ssl=1 438w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1001-1.jpg?resize=768%2C1052&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-1001-1.jpg?resize=717%2C982&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 994px) 100vw, 994px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>(It&#8217;s a <em>perfect </em>way to share photos from an event, a real-estate shoot, or even a family photo session!)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Let&#8217;s get started. </p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-choose-your-collage-photos\">Step 1: Choose your collage photos</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Before you actually <em>create </em>the collage, you&#8217;ll need to pick your collage photos &#8211; and you&#8217;ll need to do this carefully. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I recommend selecting images connected by a theme (such as a location, an event, or even a concept). Include a mix of subjects at different scales; for instance, pick some wide shots that show the entire scene, as well as some detail photos that show lots of texture and personality. Without one or the other, the story won&#8217;t be complete. And it won&#8217;t carry the level of emotion that you&#8217;re after. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Speaking of <a aria-label=\"storytelling (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/8-tips-storytelling-images/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">storytelling</a>: It often does help to focus on the story you&#8217;re trying to tell. Do you want to offer a narrative surrounding an event? Do you want to clearly convey a meaningful concept? Make sure to take this into account when picking photos!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>One more tip: If possible, include at least three photos and no more than eight. Too few photos, and you won&#8217;t be able to tell the full story. Too many photos, and you&#8217;ll confuse the viewer with clutter (plus, it&#8217;ll be tough to show off individual details).</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-open-the-selected-images-in-photoshop\">Step 2: Open the selected images in Photoshop</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Once you&#8217;ve picked your photos, open them all in Photoshop.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>To do this, you can drag and drop files directly onto the document window, or you can select <strong>File>Open</strong> and click on the relevant images.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209030\" style=\"width:570px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:570px; padding-top:172.28%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"570\" height=\"982\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-2.jpg?resize=570%2C982&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"opening your images\" class=\"wp-image-209030\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-2.jpg?w=570&#38;ssl=1 570w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-2.jpg?resize=174%2C300&#38;ssl=1 174w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-2.jpg?resize=348%2C600&#38;ssl=1 348w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 570px) 100vw, 570px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>You should see the photos as separate tabs in the document window, like this:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209031\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:75%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1125\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-3.jpg?resize=1500%2C1125&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"the collage images open in Photoshop\" class=\"wp-image-209031\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-3.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-3.jpg?resize=300%2C225&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-3.jpg?resize=600%2C450&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-3.jpg?resize=768%2C576&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-3.jpg?resize=717%2C538&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-create-a-new-file-for-your-photoshop-collage\">Step 3: Create a new file for your Photoshop collage</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Every Photoshop collage needs a background file where all the images will eventually be assembled. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>While you can use an old collage template, if you&#8217;re making your first-ever collage, you&#8217;ll need to create a new document.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So select <strong>File&#62;New </strong>in the Menu bar (or tap <em>Ctrl/Cmd+N</em>): </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209032\" style=\"width:650px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:650px; padding-top:150.77%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650\" height=\"980\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-4.jpg?resize=650%2C980&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"creating a new file\" class=\"wp-image-209032\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-4.jpg?w=650&#38;ssl=1 650w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-4.jpg?resize=199%2C300&#38;ssl=1 199w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-4.jpg?resize=398%2C600&#38;ssl=1 398w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>A New Document window should pop up, and you&#8217;ll need to dial in your file preferences. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209033\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:66.67%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-5.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting dimensions for your new file\" class=\"wp-image-209033\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-5.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-5.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-5.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-5.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-5.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-5.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>The specifics will depend on what you plan to do with the collage as well as the sizes of your chosen photos. If you&#8217;re working with big JPEGs and you aim to print, you should probably pick a 5000+ pixel width and height. If you want to display your collage on a standard web page, however, a 1500 pixel width and height will do just fine (though you can always start big and resize later, as discussed in <strong>Step 8 </strong>below).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>(I do recommend you make the file size a bit larger than the size you want in the end; that way, you can do a final crop to deal with any arrangement issues.)</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-add-your-images-one-at-a-time\">Step 3: Add your images one at a time</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Head to your first open photo, then select it. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>To do this, you can drag with the <a aria-label=\"Marquee tool (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/five-secrets-of-the-marquee-tools-in-photoshop/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Marquee tool</a>:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209034\" style=\"width:291px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:291px; padding-top:168.73%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"291\" height=\"491\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-6.jpg?resize=291%2C491&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"marquee tool how to make a Photoshop collage\" class=\"wp-image-209034\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-6.jpg?w=291&#38;ssl=1 291w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-6.jpg?resize=178%2C300&#38;ssl=1 178w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 291px) 100vw, 291px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Or you can hit <em>Ctrl/Cmd+A</em>. You should see the marching ants around the border of your image:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209035\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:69.13%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1037\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-7.jpg?resize=1500%2C1037&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selected image\" class=\"wp-image-209035\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-7.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-7.jpg?resize=300%2C207&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-7.jpg?resize=600%2C415&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-7.jpg?resize=768%2C531&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-7.jpg?resize=717%2C496&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then choose <strong>Edit&#62;Copy </strong>(or tap <em>Ctrl/Cmd+C</em>):</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209036\" style=\"width:502px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:502px; padding-top:91.24%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"502\" height=\"458\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-8.jpg?resize=502%2C458&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"copying an image\" class=\"wp-image-209036\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-8.jpg?w=502&#38;ssl=1 502w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-8.jpg?resize=300%2C274&#38;ssl=1 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 502px) 100vw, 502px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Finally, head over to the new document, then choose <strong>Edit&#62;Paste</strong> (or tap <em>Ctrl/Cmd+V</em>):</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209037\" style=\"width:514px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:514px; padding-top:84.44%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"514\" height=\"434\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-9.jpg?resize=514%2C434&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"pasting an image\" class=\"wp-image-209037\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-9.jpg?w=514&#38;ssl=1 514w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-9.jpg?resize=300%2C253&#38;ssl=1 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 514px) 100vw, 514px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>This will add the photo to the blank document, but on its own <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/photoshop-layers-for-beginners/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"layer (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">layer</a>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Depending on the size and resolution of the new image, you may need to make some adjustments with <strong>Edit&#62;Free Transform </strong>(or <em>Ctrl/Cmd+T</em>). For instance, my first photo was way too large:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209038\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:88.13%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1322\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-10.jpg?resize=1500%2C1322&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"a too-large photo how to make a Photoshop collage\" class=\"wp-image-209038\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-10.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-10.jpg?resize=300%2C264&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-10.jpg?resize=600%2C529&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-10.jpg?resize=768%2C677&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-10.jpg?resize=717%2C632&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>So I used the Free Transform option to scale it down:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209039\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:95.53%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1433\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-11.jpg?resize=1500%2C1433&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"using Free Transform\" class=\"wp-image-209039\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-11.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-11.jpg?resize=300%2C287&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-11.jpg?resize=600%2C573&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-11.jpg?resize=768%2C734&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-11.jpg?resize=717%2C685&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>(Once you&#8217;ve activated Free Transform, simply drag the edge nodes until you get the result you&#8217;re after. You want an image that&#8217;s small enough to be comfortably moved around the canvas.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Then repeat the above instructions for all the remaining collage photos.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-arrange-your-photos\">Step 4: Arrange your photos</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>After you&#8217;ve added all the collage photos to your document, it&#8217;s time to do some arranging. This is where you shift the photos around until they tell your story.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>After doing several collages, you&#8217;ll start to discover your preferred style; personally, I like to create symmetrical layouts as well as interlocking puzzles. But each story does have slightly different needs, so don&#8217;t be afraid to experiment! </p>\n\n\n\n<p>To adjust the photo positions, you can select the <strong>Move tool</strong> (or tap <em>V</em>):</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209040\" style=\"width:87px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:87px; padding-top:668.97%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"87\" height=\"582\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-12.jpg?resize=87%2C582&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"the Move tool\" class=\"wp-image-209040\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-12.jpg?w=87&#38;ssl=1 87w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-12.jpg?resize=45%2C300&#38;ssl=1 45w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 87px) 100vw, 87px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then drag around all the images until you get a good result. If you&#8217;d like to resize any photos, use the Free Transform option discussed above.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>With my pet collage example, I first tried a more symmetrical arrangement:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209041\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:69.8%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1047\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-13.jpg?resize=1500%2C1047&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"one version of the pet collage in Photoshop\" class=\"wp-image-209041\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-13.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-13.jpg?resize=300%2C209&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-13.jpg?resize=600%2C419&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-13.jpg?resize=768%2C536&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-13.jpg?resize=717%2C500&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>But I settled on a puzzle-type composition:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209042\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:94.27%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1414\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-14.jpg?resize=1500%2C1414&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"another version of the pet collage in Photoshop\" class=\"wp-image-209042\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-14.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-14.jpg?resize=300%2C283&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-14.jpg?resize=600%2C566&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-14.jpg?resize=768%2C724&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-14.jpg?resize=717%2C676&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-add-image-spacing\">Step 5: Add image spacing</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Once you&#8217;ve determined the layout and you&#8217;ve sized all the images, I recommend giving the design some space. It&#8217;s personal preference, but the effect is generally nice. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>In other words, instead of a collage like this:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209043\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:98.87%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1483\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-15.jpg?resize=1500%2C1483&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"collage without spacing\" class=\"wp-image-209043\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-15.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-15.jpg?resize=300%2C297&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-15.jpg?resize=600%2C593&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-15.jpg?resize=768%2C759&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-15.jpg?resize=717%2C709&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-15.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>You want one like this:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209044\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:96.87%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1453\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-16.jpg?resize=1500%2C1453&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"collage with spacing\" class=\"wp-image-209044\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-16.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-16.jpg?resize=300%2C291&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-16.jpg?resize=600%2C581&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-16.jpg?resize=768%2C744&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-16.jpg?resize=717%2C695&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>It&#8217;s pretty easy to do; you simply create a thin, white border between the images. You can select each photo, then use the mouse or arrow keys to drag until you see white space. Or you can double-click on each image in the Layers panel:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209045\" style=\"width:346px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:346px; padding-top:178.32%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"346\" height=\"617\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-17.jpg?resize=346%2C617&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting an image in the Layers panel\" class=\"wp-image-209045\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-17.jpg?w=346&#38;ssl=1 346w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-17.jpg?resize=168%2C300&#38;ssl=1 168w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-17.jpg?resize=336%2C600&#38;ssl=1 336w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 346px) 100vw, 346px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>This will open the <strong>Layer Style </strong>menu, where you can select the <strong>Stroke </strong>option: </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209046\" style=\"width:1175px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1175px; padding-top:59.57%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1175\" height=\"700\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-18.jpg?resize=1175%2C700&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting Stroke\" class=\"wp-image-209046\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-18.jpg?w=1175&#38;ssl=1 1175w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-18.jpg?resize=300%2C179&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-18.jpg?resize=600%2C357&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-18.jpg?resize=768%2C458&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-18.jpg?resize=717%2C427&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Make sure the Position is set to <strong>Inside</strong>, the<strong> </strong>Blend Mode is set to <strong>Normal</strong>, and the color is set to <strong>White</strong>:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209047\" style=\"width:429px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:429px; padding-top:85.08%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"429\" height=\"365\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-19.jpg?resize=429%2C365&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"adjusting the Stroke settings\" class=\"wp-image-209047\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-19.jpg?w=429&#38;ssl=1 429w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-19.jpg?resize=300%2C255&#38;ssl=1 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 429px) 100vw, 429px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then increase the <strong>Size </strong>until you see a nice border appearing around your images.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209048\" style=\"width:474px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:474px; padding-top:79.32%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"474\" height=\"376\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-20.jpg?resize=474%2C376&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"changing the Stroke size\" class=\"wp-image-209048\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-20.jpg?w=474&#38;ssl=1 474w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-20.jpg?resize=300%2C238&#38;ssl=1 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 474px) 100vw, 474px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Unfortunately, this will crop the images somewhat &#8211; but depending on the look you like, it might be worth it.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-merge-all-layers\">Step 6: Merge all layers</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>At this point, you should have your collage laid out with perfect photo spacing. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Which means you&#8217;re ready to merge all the layers. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Simply select <strong>Layer&#62;Merge Visible</strong> (or tap <em>Ctrl/Cmd+Shift+E</em>):</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209049\" style=\"width:580px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:580px; padding-top:204.14%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"580\" height=\"1184\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-21.jpg?resize=580%2C1184&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"merging visible layers how to make a Photoshop collage\" class=\"wp-image-209049\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-21.jpg?w=580&#38;ssl=1 580w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-21.jpg?resize=147%2C300&#38;ssl=1 147w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-21.jpg?resize=294%2C600&#38;ssl=1 294w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 580px) 100vw, 580px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And the layers will merge into a single beautiful Photoshop collage!</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-crop-the-final-image\">Step 7: Crop the final image</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Before you resize and export your collage, I recommend cropping any extra white space around the edges (you want the design to look even).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Just hit <em>C </em>or select the <strong><a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/5-secrets-of-the-photoshop-crop-tool/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Crop tool</a></strong>:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209050\" style=\"width:504px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:504px; padding-top:158.53%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"504\" height=\"799\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-22.jpg?resize=504%2C799&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting the Crop tool\" class=\"wp-image-209050\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-22.jpg?w=504&#38;ssl=1 504w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-22.jpg?resize=189%2C300&#38;ssl=1 189w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-22.jpg?resize=378%2C600&#38;ssl=1 378w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 504px) 100vw, 504px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then drag at the edges of the photo to get rid of any unwanted areas:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209051\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:99.33%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1490\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-23.jpg?resize=1500%2C1490&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"cropping away unwanted space\" class=\"wp-image-209051\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-23.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-23.jpg?resize=300%2C298&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-23.jpg?resize=600%2C596&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-23.jpg?resize=150%2C150&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-23.jpg?resize=768%2C763&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-23.jpg?resize=717%2C712&#38;ssl=1 717w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-23.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-resize\">Step 8: Resize</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>This step depends on your goals for the collage. If you want to print, you&#8217;ll need to resize based on printing requirements (which will generally involve leaving the image pretty large). If you want to post your collage on Facebook, Instagram, or Pinterest, however, consider sizing down to a maximum of 1500 pixels on the long end. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So select <strong>Image&#62;Image Size</strong> (or tap <em>Alt/Opt+Ctrl/Cmd+I</em>):</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209052\" style=\"width:440px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:440px; padding-top:148.86%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"440\" height=\"655\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-25.jpg?resize=440%2C655&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"adjusting the image size\" class=\"wp-image-209052\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-25.jpg?w=440&#38;ssl=1 440w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-25.jpg?resize=202%2C300&#38;ssl=1 202w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-25.jpg?resize=403%2C600&#38;ssl=1 403w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 440px) 100vw, 440px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then dial in your preferred width and height.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"step-save-and-export-your-collage\">Step 9: Save and export your collage</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Last but not least:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Save and export!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You&#8217;ll want to select <strong>File&#62;Save As</strong>:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209053\" style=\"width:443px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:443px; padding-top:97.52%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"443\" height=\"432\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-26.jpg?resize=443%2C432&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"saving your collage\" class=\"wp-image-209053\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-26.jpg?w=443&#38;ssl=1 443w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-26.jpg?resize=300%2C293&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-26.jpg?resize=50%2C50&#38;ssl=1 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 443px) 100vw, 443px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then choose a location and file name, make sure that <strong>Save as type </strong>is set to <strong>JPEG</strong>, and hit <strong>Save</strong>:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209054\" style=\"width:1180px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1180px; padding-top:95.76%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1180\" height=\"1130\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-27.jpg?resize=1180%2C1130&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"saving as a JPEG\" class=\"wp-image-209054\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-27.jpg?w=1180&#38;ssl=1 1180w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-27.jpg?resize=300%2C287&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-27.jpg?resize=600%2C575&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-27.jpg?resize=768%2C735&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-27.jpg?resize=717%2C687&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And select your preferred image quality (I usually go for around <strong>8</strong>):</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209055\" style=\"width:503px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:503px; padding-top:92.25%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"503\" height=\"464\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-28.jpg?resize=503%2C464&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"JPEG options\" class=\"wp-image-209055\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-28.jpg?w=503&#38;ssl=1 503w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-28.jpg?resize=300%2C277&#38;ssl=1 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 503px) 100vw, 503px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And you&#8217;re done! Photoshop will save your collage in the specified location. </p>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-final-words\">How to make a Photoshop collage: final words</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Well, there you have it:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>A simple process for creating a collage in Photoshop. It&#8217;s bound to look great, so don&#8217;t be shy; share it all over your social media pages!</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><span class=\"responsive-image wp-image-209056\" style=\"width:1500px\"><span class=\"space\" style=\"width:1500px; padding-top:75.4%\"></span><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1131\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-24.jpg?resize=1500%2C1131&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"the final collage in Photoshop\" class=\"wp-image-209056\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-24.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-24.jpg?resize=300%2C226&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-24.jpg?resize=600%2C452&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-24.jpg?resize=768%2C579&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/05/how-to-make-a-photoshop-collage-24.jpg?resize=717%2C541&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></span></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Now over to you:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>Have you made any collages previously? Have any additional tips? Please share your advice (and collage photos!) in the comments below.</em></p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/make-photoshop-collage-9-steps/\">How to Make a Photoshop Collage (in 9 Simple Steps)</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. It was authored by <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/author/nataliarobert/\">Natalia Robert</a>.</p>\n<div class=\"feedflare\">\n<a
